teni'one a pahela ko'i manavi athava jine hatha nathi lagavyo
basa! (He manavi'o ane jinnato) tame potana palanaharani ka'i ka'i ne'amatone juthalavaso
lila galica ane uttama patharana para takiya lagavi betha hase
basa! (He manavi'o ane jinnato) tame potana palanaharani ka'i ka'i ne'amatone juthalavaso
tara palanaharanum nama khuba ja barakatavalum che, je ijhajhatadara ane prabhavasali che
jyare kayamata avi pahoncase
jene thavamam kami jutha nathi
te (kayamata) nica karavavali ane unca karavavali hase
jyare ke dharati dharatikampa sathe halavi devamam avase
ane parvato atyanta cure cura kari devamam avase
pachi te vikherayeli mati jeva tha'i jase
ane tame trana juthomam tha'i jaso
basa! Jamana hathavala keva sara hase. Jamana hathavala
ane daba hathavalani sum dasa che, daba hathavalani
ane je agalavala che te to agalavala ja che
te khuba ja najika rahevavala hase
ne'amatovali jannatomam che
(khuba ja motum) jutha to agala rahevavala'o num hase
ane thodaka pachala loko manthi
a loko sonana tarathi banela asano para
eka-bija same takiya lagavi betha hase
te'o pase eva balako hase je'o hammesa (balako ja) rahese. Ava-ja karata hase
pyala, jaga ane evum jama la'ine je vaheti
jenathi na to mathamam dukhavo thase, na to budhdhi niskriya thase
ane eva phalo la'ine je te'one managamata hase
ane pankhi'ona gosta je te'one pasanda hase
ane moti moti ankhovali apsara'o
Je chupayela moti'o jevi hase
a badalo che temana karmono
na tyam phalatum vata sambhalase ane na to papani vata
phakata salama ja salamani avaja hase
ane jamana hathavala ketala uttama che. Jamana hathavala'o
te'o kanta vagara
ane eka pachi eka khunta
ane lamba lamba padachaya
ane vaheta pani
ane ghana ja phalomam
je na to khatma thase, na to roki levamam avase
ane unca unca patharana para hase
ame te'o (ni patni'one) khasa tarikathi banavi che
ane ame teni'one kumarika'o banavi didhi che
mohabbata karanari ane sarakhi vayo vali
jamana hathavala'o mate che
ghana loko agala rahevavala loko manthi hase
ane ghanum ja motum jutha pachala rahevavala'onum che
ane daba hathavala, keva che daba hathavala
garama hava ane garama pani mam (hase)
ane kala dhumadana padachayamam
je na to thando hase ane na to khusa karanaro
ni:Sanka a loko a pahela ghana ja thathamam hata
ane mota mota gunaha para adaga raheta
ane kaheta hata sum ame mrtyu pamisum, mati ane hadaka tha'i ja'isum to sum ame pacha bijivara jivita karavamam avisum
ane sum amara agalana bapa-dada'o pana
tame kahi do ke ni:Sanka agala ane pachalana saune
jarurathi bhega kari devamam avase, eka nakki karela divase
pachi tame he pathabhrasto! He juthalavanara'o
tame jarurathi
ane tenathi ja tame peta bharaso
pachi tena para garama ukalatum pani piso
pivavala pana tarasya unto jeva
kayamatana divase te'oni a mahemani hase
ame ja tamara saunum sarjana karyum che. Pachi tame kema manata nathi
Ha, evum to janavo ke je virya tame tapakavo cho
sum tene (manavi) tame banavo cho? Athava to peda karanara ame ja che
ame ja tamara para mrtyune nakki kari didhu che. Ane ame tenathi harela nathi
ke tamari jagya para tamara jeva ketalayane peda kari da'i'e ane tamane pharithi a jagatamam pana peda kari da'i'e jeni tamane kami pana khabara nathi
tamane nisrcitapane pahela sarjana vise khabara ja che, pachi kema bodha grahana nathi karata
ha to e pana janavo ke tame je kami pana vavo cho
teni vavani tame ja karo cho athava to ame ja vavetara che
jo ame icchi'e to tene cure cura kari da'i'e ane tame asrcaryathi vato ghadavamam ja rahi ja'o
ke amara para bhara tha'i gayo che
parantu ame khuba ja ajana rahi gaya
ha e to janavo ke je pani tame pivo cho
tene vadalo manthi tame ja utaro cho athava to ame utari'e chi'e
jo amari iccha hoya to ame tene kadavum jhera banavi da'i'e. Pachi tame amaro abhara kema nathi manata
ham e pana janavo ke je aga tame salagavo cho
tena vuksane tame peda karyu che athava ame tene peda karavavala che
ame tene sikhamana mate ane musapharona phayada mate banavyum che
basa! Potana ghana ja mahanatavala palanaharana namanum smarana karata raho
basa! Hum soganda kha'um chum tara'ona padavana
ane jo tamane jnana hoya to a ghani ja moti soganda che
ni:Sanka a kura'ana khuba ja ijajatavalum che
je eka suraksita pustakamam che
tene phakata pavitra loko ja adi sake che
a jagatana palanahara taraphathi avatarita karelum che
sum tame a vatane saman'ya jano cho
ane potana bhagamam phakata juthalavavanum ja nakki karyum che
Basa! Jyare jiva gala sudhi pahonci jase
ane tame te samaye ankho vade jota rahi jaso
ame te vyakti sathe tamara karata vadhare najika ho'i'e chi'e, parantu tame nathi jo'i sakata
basa! Jo tame ko'ina kahevamam nathi
ane jo a vatana saca hoya to a jivane pache lavi bata'o
basa! Je ko'i allahana darabaramam najika karelo hase
tene to arama che, khoraka che ane aramadayaka jannata che
ane je vyakti jamana (hatha) vala'o manthi che
to pana salamati che tara mate ke tum jamana hathavala'o manthi che
parantu jo ko'i juthalavanara pathabhrasto manthi che
tena mate ukalata garama panini mahemani che
ane jahannamamam javanum che
a khabara kharekhara saci ane satya che
basa! Tum potana mahana palanaharana namanum smarana kara
akaso ane dharatimam je kami pana che (badhum ja) allahana namanum smarana kari rahya che, te mahana, hikamatavalo che
akaso ane dharatinum samrajya tenum ja che. Te ja jivana ape che ane te ja mrtyu pana ane te dareka vastu para saktimana che
te ja prathama che ane te ja chelle che, te ja jhahira che ane te ja chupo ane te dareka vastune khuba ja sari rite jane che
te (allaha) ja che jene akaso ane dharatinum cha divasamam sarjana karyu, pachi arsa para birajamana tha'i gayo, te (khuba ja) jane che te vastune je jaminamam jaya ane je temanthi nikale ane je akasa parathi nice ave ane je kami cadhine jaya ane jyam pana tame cho te tamari sathe che ane je kami pana tame kari rahya cho (tene) allaha jo'i rahyo che
akaso ane dharatinum samrajya tenum ja che ane dareka karya teni ja tarapha mokalavamam ave che
Te ja ratrine divasamam pherave che ane te ja divasane ratrimam pherave che ane hrdayona bhedone te khuba ja sari rite jane che
allaha ane tena payagambara para imana lavi do ane dhana manthi kharca karo jemam allaha'e tamane (bijana) labharthi banavya che. Basa! Tamara manthi je imana lave ane dana kare tene puskala savaba (punya) malase
tame allaha para imana kema nathi lavata? Jyare ke payagambara pote tamane potana palanahara para imana lavavanum kahe che ane jo tame imanavala hoya to te to tamarathi thosa vacana pana la'i cukaya che
te (allaha) ja che je potana banda para spasta ayato utare che, jethi te tamane andhakarathi prakasa tarapha la'i jaya. Ni:Sanka allaha ta'ala tamara para namrata karanara ane daya karanara che
tamane sum tha'i gayum che ke tame allahana margamam dana nathi karata? Asalamam akaso ane dharatini varasa'i no malika (ekalo) allaha ja che, tamara manthi je loko'e vijaya pahela allahana margamam dana karyu che ane yudhdha karyu che te'o (bijana) jeva nathi, parantu te'o temana karata uttama darajjavala che, jemane vijaya pachi dana karyu ane jehada karyu. Ham sara karmonum vacana allaha'e te saune karelum che. Je kami pana tame kari rahya cho tene allaha khuba sari rite jane che
kona che je allaha ta'alane sari rite udhara ape, pachi allaha ta'ala tene tena mate vadharato jaya che ane tena mate manapasanda badalo nakki tha'i jaya
(kayamatana) divase tame jo'i leso ke imanavala puruso ane stri'ono prakasa temana agala agala ane te'ona jamane dodi rahyu hase. Aje tamane te jannatoni subhasucana che jeni nice nahero vaheti che, jemam hammesanu avasa che, a che moti saphalata
Te divase dhongi purusa ane stri imanavala'one kahese ke amari pratiksa to karo, ke ame pana tamara prakasathi kami prakasa melavi la'i'e, javaba apavamam avase ke tame potani pachala phari java ane prakasa sodho, pachi te banneni vacce eka divala kari devamam avase, jemam baranum pana hase, tena andarana bhagamam ananda hase ane baharana bhagamam yatana hase
a loko rado padine temane (jannati'o ne) kahese ke sum ame tamari sathe na hata, te'o kahese ke ha hata to khara pana tame pote vidrohi bani gaya hata ane pratiksa karavamam ja rahi gaya ane sanka karata rahya ane tamane tamara bekarana sokho'e dhoka mam ja rakhya, tyam sudhi ke allahano adesa avi pahoncyo ane tamane allaha vise dhoko apanare dhoka mam ja rakhya
basa! Aje tamari pase na to???? (Ane na to badalo) kabula karavamam avase ane na inkari'othi, tamara (sau) num thekanum jahannama che, te ja tamari dosta che ane te ghanum ja kharaba thekanum che
sum haju sudhi imanavala'o mate samaya nathi avyo ke te'ona hrdayo allahani yadamam ane je satya marga avatarita tha'i cukayo che tenathi narama tha'i jaya ane temana jeva na tha'i jaya jemane te pahela grantha apavamam avyo hato pachi jyare te'o para eka lambo galo pasara tha'i cukayo to temana hrdayo sakhata tha'i gaya ane temanamam ghanaja vidrohi che
kharekhara tame jani lo ke allaha ja dharatine tena mrtyu pachi phari jivita kari de che, ame to tamara mate amari ayatonum varnana kari didhum jethi tame samaji lo
ni:Sanka dana karavavala puruso ane stri'o ane je allahane nikhalasatathi udhara api rahya che te'o mate te vadharavamam avase, ane te'o mate manapasanda savaba che
Allaha ane tena payagambara para je imana rakhe che te ja loko potana palanaharani najika saca ane sahida che, te'o mate te'ono badalo ane te'o mate prakasa che ane je loko inkara kare che ane amari ayatone juthalave che te jahannami che
jani lo ke duniyanum jivana phakata ramata-gamata, sanagara ane eka- bijamam ahankara ane dhana tatha santano babate eka bijana dekhadekhimam potane srestha batavavanum che, jevi rite ke varasada ane teni pedavara khedutone lubhave che, pachi jyare te suki padi jaya che to pila rangamam tame tene ju'o cho, pachi te cure cura tha'i jaya che. Ane akheratamam sakhata yatana ane allahani maphi ane rajamandi che, ane duniyanum jivana phakata dhoko ja che, te vagara kami nathi
(avo) bhago potana palanaharani ksama tarapha ane teni jannato tarapha teni coda'i akasa ane dharatini coda'i jetali che, a te loko mate taiyara karavamam avi che je allaha ane tena payagambaro para imana dharave che. A allahani krpa che jene icche ape ane allaha ghano ja krpalu che
ko'i musibata tamane ane tamara jivone duniyamam nathi pahoncati parantu te pahela ke ame tene peda kari'e, te eka khasa pustakamam lakheli che, a (karya) allaha mate (khuba ja) sarala che
jethi tame na maleli vastu para ranja na karo ane na to apeli vastu para itara'o ane ahankari'one allaha pasanda nathi karato
je kanjusi kare ane bijane (pana) kanjusini sikhamana ape, sambhalo je pana modhum pherave allaha beniyajha ane prasansane layaka che
Ni:Sanka ame amara payagambarone khulla purava api mokalya ane teni sathe pustaka ane trajavum avatarita karyu, jethi loko n'yaya para adaga rahe ane ame lokhanda utaryu jemam sakhata'i ane takata che, ane loko mate bija ghanam phayada che ane a mate pana ke allaha jani le ke teni ane tena payagambaroni madada vana dekhe kona kare che, ni:Sanka allaha takatavara ane mahana che
ni:Sanka ame nuha ane ibrahima (a.Sa.) Ne (payagambara banavi) mokalya ane ame te banneni santanomam payagambari ane grantho paramparita rakhya, to temanthi ketalake to satya marga apanavyo ane temanthi ghana ja avajnakari rahya
tyara pachi pana ame amara payagambarone eka pachi eka mokalta rahya, ane te pachi isa bina marayama (a.Sa.) Ne mokalya, ane temane injila api ane temana mananara'ona hrdayomam daya ane namrata peda kari didhi, ham rahabaniyyata (san'yasi) to te loko'e pote banavi didhi, ame te'ona para jaruri nahatu theravyu, allahani raja sivaya, to te loko'e tenum pure puru palana na karyu, to pana ame te'ona manthi je imana lavya hata te'one teno badalo apyo ane temanamam ghana loko avajnakari hata
he loko je'o imana lavya cho allahathi darata raho, ane tena payagambara para imana lavo, allaha tamane potani krpano bamano bhaga apase, ane tamane prakasa apase, jena prakasamam tame hari- phari sakaso ane tamara gunaha pana mapha kari dese, allaha ksama karanara, dayalu che
a etala mate ke granthavala'o jani le ke allahani krpana ko'i bhagamam pana te'one kami adhikara nathi, ane (dareka) krpa allahana ja hathamam che, te jene icche ape, ane allaha che ja ghano krpalu
Ni:Sanka allaha ta'ala'e te strini vata sambhali je tarathi potana pati babata rakajhaka kari rahi hati ane allaha ta'alathi phariyada kari rahi hati. Allaha ta'ala tamara bannena prasrnottara sambhali rahyo hato. Ni:Sanka allaha ta'ala sambhalavavalo, jovavalo che
tamara manthi je loko potani patni'o sathe jhihara (etale ke potani patnine mam jevi kahevum) kare che te kharekhara temani mam nathi bani jati, temani mam to te ja che jemana petathi te'o peda thaya, ni:Sanka a loko eka bekara ane juthi vata kahe che. Ni:Sanka allaha ta'ala ksama karavavalo che
je loko potani patni'othi jhihara kare, pachi potani kaheli vatathi pacha phare to temana para eka bijane hatha lagavatam pahela eka dasane ajhada karavo padase, tena vade tamane sikhamana apavamam ave che. Ane allaha ta'ala tamara dareka karyone khuba jane che
ham, je vyakti (dasa ajhada karavani) ksamata na dharavato hoya to tena para be masana lagalagata rojha che. Te pahela ke eka bijane hatha lagave, ane je vyaktine teni ksamata pana na dharave tena para sahitha lacarone khavanum khavadavavanum che, a etala mate ke tame allaha ane tena payagambarana adesanum palana karo, a allaha ta'alani nakki karela maryada'o che ane inkari'o mate ja du:Khadayi yatana che
ni:Sanka je loko allaha ane tena payagambarano virodha kare che te apamanita karavamam avase, jemake athi pahelana lokone apamanita karavamam avya ane ni:Sanka ame khulli ayato utari cukaya che ane inkari'o mate to apamanita kari denari yatana che
Je divase allaha ta'ala te dareka lokone jivita karase. Phari temane temana karela karyothi khabaradara karase, jene allaha e gani- ganine suraksita rakhya ane jene te bhuli gaya hata, ane allaha ta'ala dareka vastuthi khuba ja vakepha che
sum tame nathi joyum ke allaha akasoni ane dharatini dareka vastuthi vakepha che. Trana manavi'oni vatacita nathi thati parantu allaha temanthi cotho hoya che ane pancani parantu temanthi chaththo te hoya che ane tenathi ochani ane vadhareni parantu te sathe ja hoya che, jyam pana te'o hoya. Phari kayamatana divase temane temana karyothi khabaradara karase, ni:Sanka allaha ta'ala dareka vastuthi vakepha che
sum tame te lokone nathi joya? Je lokone gusapusa karavathi rokavamam avya hata, te'o rokava chatam te karyane pharivara kare che ane te'o andara-andara papa, atireka ane payagambarani avajnani gusapusa kare che ane jyare tamari pase ave che to tamane te sabdo vade salama kare che je sabdomam allaha ta'ala'e nathi kahyum ane potana manamam kahe che ke allaha ta'ala amane tena para je ame kahi rahya che siksa kema nathi api rahyo, temana mate jahannama purati che, jemam te'o jase. To te ghanum ja kharaba thekanum che
he imanavala'o! Tame jyare vatacita karo to a vatacita gunaha, atireka ane payagambarani avajna tarapha (ubharati) na hoya, parantu bhala'i ane sayammani vatacita karo ane allahathi darata raho, jeni pase tame sau bhega karavamam avaso
gusapusa e to eka setani kama che jenathi imanavalone thesa pahonce. Joke allaha ta'alani iccha vagara temane ko'i thesa pahoncadi sakatum nathi. Ane imanavala'o allaha para ja visrvasa rakhe
He musalamano! Jyare tamane kahevamam ave ke sabha'omam thoda khulla beso to tame khulla besi java, jethi allaha tamane(dareka vastu'omam) vadhare apase, ane jyare kahevamam ave ke ubha tha'i java to tame ubha tha'i java, allaha ta'ala tamara manthi te lokona, je imana vala'o che ane jemane jnana apavamam avyum che, darajja'o unca kari dese ane allaha ta'ala (dareka karyathi) je tame kari rahya cho (khuba ja) vakepha che
he musalamano! Jyare tame payagambarathi vatacita karava iccho to potani vatacita pahela kamika sadako (dana) api do a tamara mate uttama ane pavitra che, ham jo tame (sadako) na pamo to, ni:Sanka allaha ta'ala ksama karanara ane dayalu che
sum tame potani vatacita pahela sadako apavathi dari gaya? Basa jyare tame avum na karyu ane allaha ta'ala'e pana tamane mapha kari didha to have (khuba ja sari rite) namajha hammesa padhata raho, jhakata apata raho ane allaha ta'alani ane tena payagambaranum ajnapalana karata raho, tame je kami pana karo cho te (badha thi) allaha (khuba ja) janakara che
sum tame te lokone nathi joya? Jemane te koma sathe mitrata kari jena para allaha khuba ja gus'se tha'i cukayo che, na to a (dhongi) tamara che ane na temana che, janava chatam juthi vato para sogando kha'i rahya che
allaha ta'ala e temana mate sakhata yatana taiyara kari rakhi che, kharekhara je (krtyo) te'o kari rahya che kharaba kari rahya che
te loko'e to potani sogandone ada banavi rakhi che ane lokone allahana margathi roki rahya che temana mate apamanajanaka yatana che
temanum dhana ane santano allaha pase kami ja kama nahim ave, a loko jahannami che. Hammesa temam ja rahese
Je divase allaha ta'ala te darekane jivita karase to a loko jevi rite tamari same sogando khaya che, (allaha ta'ala) ni same pana sogando khava lagase ane samajase ke te'o pase pana ko'i (purava) che, barabara jani lo ke, ni:Sanka te'o ja jutha che
temana para setana chava'i gayo che ane temane allaha na smaranathi vancita kari didha che, a setani jutha che, ko'i sanka nathi ke setani jutha ja nukasanamam che
ni:Sanka allaha ta'ala ane tena payagambarano je loko virodha kare che te ja loko sauthi vadhare apamanita che
allaha ta'ala lakhi cukayo che ke ni:Sanka hum ane maro payagambara ja navijayi rahisum, ni:Sanka allaha ta'ala ja saktisali ane vijayi che
allaha ta'ala ane kiyamatana divasa para imana rakhanara'one allaha ane tena payagambarana virodhi'o sathe mohabbata karata tame nahim ju'o, bhalene pachi temana pita, dikara ane bha'i athava temana kuntubi'o pana kema na hoya, a ja loko che jemana hrdayomam allaha ta'ala'e imana lakhi didhum che. Ane jeni pusti potani ruha vade kari che. Ane jemane te jannatomam dakhala karase jemani jice nahero vahi rahi che. Jyam te'o hammesa rahese, allaha temanathi khusa che ane a allahathi khusa che. A allahanum jutha che. Savadhana raho kharekhara allaha na juthavala'o ja saphala loko che
akaso ane dharatini dareka vastu'o allaha ta'ala ni pavitratanum varnana kare che, te prabala ane hikamatavalo che
Te ja che jene granthavalo manthi inkari'one, temana gharo manthi prathama cukadana samaye kadhi mukaya, tamari kalpana (pana) na hati ke te'o nikalase ane te'o pote (pana) samaji rahya hata ke temana (majabuta) killa te'one allaha (ni yatana) thi bacavi lese, basa! Te'ona para allaha (ni yatana) evi jagya'ethi avi pahonci ke temane kalpana pana na hati, ane temana hrdayomam allaha'e dara nakhi didho, te'o potana gharone potana ja hatho vade virana kari rahya hata ane musalamanona hatho vade (barabada karavi rahya hata), basa! He jonara'o siksa grahana karo
ane jo allaha ta'ala'e te'ona para desanikalane lakhi na didhum hota to cokkasa pane te'one duniyamam ja saja apato, ane akheratamam (to) te'o mate agani saja to che ja
a etala mate ke te'o'e allaha ta'ala ane tena payagambara virodha karyo ane je pana allaha no virodha karase to allaha ta'ala pana sakhata saja apanara che
tame khajurona je vrkso kapi nakhya athava jemane tame potana muliya upara baki raheva didha, a badhum ja allahana adesa pramane hatum ane etala mate pana ke papi'one allaha apamanita kare
ane te'onum je dhana allaha ta'ala'e potana payagambarana hathe pahoncadayum che jena para na to tame potana ghoda dodavya ane na unto, parantu allaha ta'ala potana payagambarane jena para icche vijayi banavi de che ane allaha ta'ala dareka vastu para saktimana che
Vasti'ovala'onum je (dhana) allaha ta'ala tamara mutha-bheda vagara potana payagambarane pahoncadayum te allahanum che, payagambara mate ane saga- sabandhi'o mate ane anatho lacaro mate ane musapharo mate che, jethi tamara dhanavanona hathamam ja a dhana pharatum na rahi jaya ane tamane payagambara je kami pana ape la'i lo, ane jenathi roke ruki java ane allaha ta'alathi darata raho, ni:Sanka allaha ta'ala sakhata saja apanara che
(jangamam ladaya vagara hatha lagela mala) te hijarata karanara lacaro mate che je potana gharabara anesampatti'o thi kadhi mukavamam avya, te allahani krpa ane prasannata icche che, te'o allaha ane tena payagambarani madada kare che, a loko ja satyanistha che
ane (temana mate pana che) je loko'e te gharamam etale ke (madina sahera) ane imana mam te lokothi (hijarata karanara'o na agamana) pahela jagya banavi didhi che ane potani tarapha hijarata kari avanara lokothi mohabbata rakhe che ane hijarata karavavala'one je kami apavamam ave tenathi te'o potana hrdayomam tangi rakhata nathi, parantu potana para te'one prathamikata ape che, cahe potani jarurata kema na hoya, (vata a che) ke je pana potana jiva mate kanjusi karavathi bacavi levamam avyo te ja saphala che
ane (temana mate pana che) je temana pachi avya, te'o kahese ke he! Amara palanahara amane mapha kari de ane amara te bha'ine pana je amara pahela imana lavi cukaya che ane imanavala'o pratye amara hrdayomam vera (ane dusmani) peda na kara, he! Amara palanahara ni:Sanka tum mayalu ane dayalu che
Sum tame dhongi'one na joya? Te potana grathavala inkari bha'i'one kahe che jo tame desanikala karavamam avya to jarurathi ame pana tamari sathe nikali ja'isum ane tamara vise ame kayareya ko'ini pana vata nahi mani'e ane jo tamarathi lada'i karavamam avase to jarurathi ame tamari madada karisu parantu allaha ta'ala saksi ape che ke a taddana jutha che
jo te lokone desanikala karavamam ave to a loko temani sathe nahi jaya ane jo temani sathe lada'i karavamam ave to a loko temani madada (pana) nahim kare ane jo (kadaca) madada karava mate avi pana gaya to pitha batavine bhagi jase, pachi madada karavamam nahim ave
(musalamano bharoso rakho) ke tamaro dara te'ona hrdayomam allahana darathi vadhare che, a etala mate ke te'o samaja-bujha dharavata nathi
a sau bhega tha'ine pana tamari sathe ladi nathi sakata, ham e vata alaga che ke killamam hoya athava divalo pachala chupayela hoya, temani lada'i to adanra adanra ja khuba che, tame temane bhega samajo cho parantu temana hrdayo asala mam ekabijathi alaga che, etala mate ke a loko samaja- bujha dharavata nathi
te lokoni jema je thodaka samaya pahela hata, jemane potana karatutono svada cakhi lidho ane jemana mate du:Khadayi yatana che
setana ni maphaka, ke tene manavi'one kahyu ke inkara kara, jyare tene (manavi'e) inkara kari didho to kaheva lagyo hum to tarathi alago chum, hum to allaha jagatana palanaharathi daru chum
basa! Banne (setana ane inkari'o) num parinama evum thayum ke jahannamamam hammesa mate gaya ane atyacari'o mate avi ja saja che
He imanavala'o! Allahathi darata raho ane dareka vyakti jo'i le ke kala (kiyamata) mate tene (karyonum) sum (sangraha) mokalyum che. Ane (dareka samaye) allahathi darata raho, allaha tamara dareka karyothi khabaradara che
ane tame te loko jeva na tha'i ja'o jemane allaha (na adeso) ne bhulavi betha, to allaha'e pana temana astitvane bhulavi didhum ane ava ja loko avajnakari hoya che
jahannamavala'o ane jannatavala'o sarakha nathi, je jannatavala'o che te ja saphala che (ane je jahannamavala che te nisphala che)
jo ame a kura'anane ko'i parvata para avatarita karata to tame jota ke allahana bhayathi te daba'ine tukade tukada tha'i jato, ame ava udaharanone loko same varnana kari'e chi'e jethi te'o cintana kare
te ja allaha che jena sivaya ko'i bandagine layaka nathi, adrasya ane drasyane janavavalo, krpalu ane atyanta dayalu
te ja allaha che jena sivaya ko'i bandagine layaka nathi, badasaha, atyanta pavitra, dareka khamithi salamata, santi apanara, dekharekha karanara, vijayi, saktisali, mota'ivalo. Pavitra che allaha, te vastu'othi jemane te'o allahana bhagidara therave che
te ja allaha che, sarjana karanara, banavanara, svarupa apanara, tena mate ja pavitra nama che, dareka vastu cahe te akasomam hoya athava to dharatimam. Teni pavitratanum varnana kare che. Ane te ja vijayi, hikamatavalo che
He imanavala'o! Mara ane (tamara) potana dusmanone potana mitra na banavo, tame to mitratathi temane sandeso mokalavo cho, ane te'o te satya vatane juthalave che je tamari pase avi ga'i che, payagambara ane tamane potane pana phakata etala mate ja desanikala kare che ke tame potana palanahara para imana dharavo cho, jo tame mara margamam jehada ane mari prasannata mate nikalo cho (to te'o sathe mitrata na rakho) tame te'one chupi chupine mohabbatano sandeso mokalavo cho ane hum khuba ja janu chum je tame chupavyum ane te pana je tame khullu karyum, tamaramanthi je ko'i avum karya karase te kharekhara satya margathi bhataki jase
jo te'o tamara upara kabu melavi le to te'o tamara (khulla) satru tha'i jase ane bura'i sathe tamane potana hatho ane jabana vade takalipha apase ane (dilathi) icchase ke tame pana inkara karava lago
tamara saga-sabandhi'o ane santano tamane kayamatana divasane kama nahim ave, te (allaha ta'ala) tamari vacce phensalo kari dese ane je kami pana tame kari rahya cho tene allaha khuba sari rite jo'i rahyo che
(Musalamano) tamara mate hajharate ibrahima ane temana sathi'omam uttama adarsa che, jyare ke te'o'e potani komathi khullu kahim didhu ke ame tamarathi ane jemani pana tame allahana sivaya bandagi kari rahya cho te badhathi taddana alipta chi'e, ame tamara (sradhdha'ona) inkari che, jyam sudhi tame ekesrvaravada para imana na lavo, amara ane tamaramam hammesa mate vera ane dusmani ubhi tha'i ga'i, parantu ibrahimani etali vatato potana pita sathe tha'i hati ke hum tamara mate jarura maphi mangisa ane tamara mate allaha same mane ko'i pana vastuno kami adhikara nathi. He amara palanahara tara para ja ame bharoso karyo ane ame tari ja tarapha pratyagamana kari'e chi'e ane tari ja tarapha pacha pharavanum che
he amara palanahara! Tum amane inkari'oni kasotimam na nakha ane he amaru palana-posana karanara! Amari bhulone mapha kari de, ni:Sanka tu ja vijayi, hikamata valo che
ni:Sanka tamara mate amam uttama adarsa (ane uttama anusarana che, khasa karine) te pratyeka vyakti mate je allaha ane kayamatana divase malavani asa rakhato hoya, ane jo ko'i avaganana kare to allaha ta'ala be niyajha che ane prasansane layaka che
sakya che ke najikamam ja allaha ta'ala tamane ane tamara dusmanomam prema nakhi de, allahane dareka sakti che ane allaha (moto) ksama karanara ane dayalu che
je loko'e tamarathi dina vise lada'i na kari ane tamane desanikala na karya temani sathe sadavartana ane n'yaya karavathi allaha tamane nathi rokato, parantu allaha to n'yaya karavavalathi mohabbata kare che
Allaha ta'ala tamane phakata te loko sathe mitrata karavathi roke che jemane tamari sathe dina babate yudhdho karya ane tamane desanikala kari didha ane desanikala karavavala'oni madada kari je loko ava inkari'o sathe mitrata rakhe che te (kharekhara) atyacari che
he imanavala'o! Jyare tamari pase imanavali stri'o hijarata karine ave to tame temani pariksa lo, karanake temana imanane khuba sari rite janavavalo to allaha ja che, parantu jo tamane imanavali lage to have tame teni'one inkari'o pase pacha na mokalo, a te'o mate halala nathi ane na te'o teni'o mate halala che ane je kharca thayo hoya te temane api do, te stri'one temani mahera api temani sathe lagna karavamam ko'i papa nathi ane inkari stri'one lagna mate roki na rakho ane je kami tame kharca karyo hoya, mangi lo ane je kami te inkari'o kharca karyo hoya te pana mangi le, a allaha no adesa che je tamara vacce kari rahyo che, allaha ta'ala badhu jananara (ane) hikamatavalo che
ane jo tamari ko'i patni tamari pasethi inkari'o pase jati rahe, pachi tamane jo badalo leva mate samaya male to jemani patni'o jati rahi che temane temano kharca api do ane te allaha ta'alathi darata raho jena para tame imana rakho cho
he payagambara! Jyare musalamana stri'o tamari pase te vato vise pratijna kare ke te'o allaha sathe ko'ine bhagidara nahim therave, cori nahim kare, vyabhicara nahim kare, potani santanone katla nahim kare ane ko'i evo aropa nahim muke je potana hatho ane pago same ghadelo hoya ane ko'i sadakaryamam tamari avajna nahim kare to tame emanathi pratijna la'i lo ane temana mate allahathi ksama mango, ni:Sanka allaha ta'ala ksama karanaravalo ane dayalu che
He muslmano! Evi koma sathe mitrata na karo jena para allahano prakopa avi cukayo che. Je akhiratathi evi rite nirasa tha'i cukaya che jevum ke (mrta) kabaravala'othi inkariyo nirasa che
dharati ane akasoni dareka dareka vastu'o allaha ta'alani pavitratanum varnana kari rahi che ane te ja vijayi ane hikamatavalo che
he imanavala'o! Tame te vata kema kaho cho je (pote) karata nathi
tame je karata nathi te kahevum, allaha ta'alane sakhata napasanda che
ni:Sanka allaha ta'ala te lokone pasanda kare che je loko tena margamam katarabandha jehada kare che. Jevum ke sisu pigalayeli divala hoya
ane (yada karo) jyare ke musa'e potani komane kahyum he mari komana loko! Tame mane kema satavi rahya cho jyare ke tame (khuba sari rite) jano cho ke hum tamari samaksa allahano payagambara chum. Basa jyare te loko ada ja rahya to allaha'e temana dilone (vadhare) ada kari didha ane allaha ta'ala avajnakari lokone saco marga nathi apato
ane jyare marayama na putra isa'e kahyum he (mari koma) bani isra'ila! Hum tamara dareka loko tarapha allahano payagambara chum, a pahelanum pustaka tauratane hum samarthana apum chum ane mara pachi avanara eka payagambarani hum tamane subha sucana apanaro chum, jenum nama ahamada che, pachi jyare te temani pase khulla purava lavya to kaheva lagya ke a to khullu jadu che
te vyaktithi vadhare atyacari kona hase je allaha para juthu ghade,jyare ke te islama tarapha bolavavamam ave che ane allaha ava atyacari'one satya marga nathi apato
te icche che ke allahana prakasa ne potana modha vade olavi dem ane allaha potana prakasa ne sampurna karine ja rahese, bhale inkari'one kharaba lage
Te ja che jene potana payagambarane satya marga ane saco gharma apine mokalya, jethi temane dareka gharmo para vijeta banavi de, bhalene (allahana) bhagidara theravanara raji na hoya
he imanavala'o! Sum hum tamane te vepara batavum je tamane du:Khadayi yatanathi bacavi le
allaha ta'ala ane tena rasula para imana lavo ane allahana margamam potanum dhana ane tana vade jihada karo a tamara mate uttama che jo tame janata hova
allaha ta'ala tamara gunaha mapha kari dese ane tamane te jannatomam pahoncadase jena nice nahero vahi rahi hase ane cokhkha gharomam je jannata adda na (jannatana namomanthi eka nama) mam hase, a khuba bhavya saphalata che
ane tamane eka biji (ne'amata) pana apase jene tame iccho cho, te allahani madada ane jhadapi vijaya che, imanavala'one subha sucana api do
he imanavala'o! Tame allaha ta'alana madada karanara bani java, jevi rite marayamana dikara isa e potana sathi'one kahyum, kona che je allahana margamam maro madada karanara bane? Sathi'o'e kahyum ame allahana margamam madada karanara che, basa! Bani isra'ilamanthi eka jutha imana lavyo ane eka juthe inkara karyo. To ame mominone te satru'ona virudhdha madada kari, basa! Te'o vijayi tha'i gaya
(dareka vastu'o) je akaso ane dharati para che allaha ta'alani pavitratanum varnana kare che, (je) badasaha, atyanta pavitra (che). Vijayi ane hikamatavalo che
te ja che jene abhana lokomam temana manthi ja eka payagambara mokalya je te'one a (kura'ana) ni ayato sambhalave che ane temane pavitra kare che ane te'one kitaba (kura'ana) tatha hikamata sikhavade che, ni:Sanka te'o a pahela khulli pathabhrastatamam hata
Ane bija mate pana temana manthi je'o atyara sudhi temane nathi malya, ane te ja vijayi ane hikamatavalo che
a allahani krpa che jena para icche tena para potani krpa kare ane allaha ta'ala ghani ja moti krpa'ono malika che
je lokone torata num anusarana karavanum kahyum pachi te'o'e tenum anusarana na karyu temanum udaharana te gadheda jevi che jene ghani ja pustako uthaveli hoya. Allahani vatone juthalavavavala'o mate ghanum kharaba udaharana che. Ane allaha (avi) atyacari komane margadarsana apato nathi
kahim do ke he yahudi'o! Jo tame evum vicarata hoya ke bija sivaya tame allahana dosta cho to tame mrtyuni iccha karo jo tame sacca hoya
a loko kadapi mrtyuni iccha nahim kare, je karyo te'o'e potana hatha vade'agala mokalya che. Ane atyacari'one khuba ja jane che
kahim do ke je mrtyuthi tame bhagata pharo cho te to tamane avine ja rahese, pachi tame dareka chupi tatha khulli (vato) no jananara (allaha) ni tarapha pacha pheravavamam avaso. Ane te tamara karela dareka karyo batavi dese
he imanavala'o! Jumahana divase namajha mate ajhana apavamam ave to tame allahana smarana tarapha bhago ane le-veca chodi do, a tamara mate khuba ja uttama che jo tame janata hova
pachi jyare namajha puri tha'i jaya to dharati para phela'i java ane allahani krpane sodho ane vadhare mam vadhare allahanum smarana karata raho, jethi tame saphalata melavi lo
ane jyare ko'i sodo thata jove athava ko'i tamaso jove to teni tarapha bhage che ane tamane ubha rahela chodi de che, tame kahim do ke allaha pase je che te ramata ane dhandhathi uttama che ane allaha ta'ala uttama roji apanara che
Tamari pase jyare munaphiko (dhongi'o) ave che to kahe che ke ame a vatani saksi api'e chi'e ke ni:Sanka tame allahana payagambara cho, ane allaha jane che ke kharekhara tame allahana payagambara cho ane allaha saksi ape che ke a munaphiko taddana jutha che
te'o'e potani sogandone dhala banavi rakhi che, basa! Allahana margathi ruki gaya, ni:Sanka kharaba che te karya je te'o kari rahya che
a etala mate ke a loko imana lavine inkari tha'i gaya, basa! Te'ona hrdayo upara mohara mari devamam avi, have a loko nathi samajata
jyare tame temane jo'i lo to temana sarira tamane sanadara lage che, a loko jyare vato karava lage to tame temani vato sambhalo, jemake te'o divalana teke rakheli lakadi'o che, dareka (sakhata) avajane potana virudhdha samaje che, a ja kharekhara dusmano che, temanathi baco, allaha te'one nasta kare, kayam avala pheravavamam avi rahya che
ane jyare te'one kahevamam ave che ke avo tamara mate allahanapayagambara ksama mange, to potana matha halave che ane tame joso ke te ghammada karata ruki jaya che
temani mate tamari ksama mangavi ane na mangavi banne barabara che, allahata'ala te'one kadapi mapha nahim kare. Ni:Sanka allaha ta'ala (ava) avajnakari lokone satyamarga nathi apato
a ja te loko che je'o kahe che ke je loko payagambara sathe che te'ona para kami kharca na karo ahim sudhi ke te'o vikheraya jaya, ane akasa ane dharatina badha khajana allahani malikina che, parantu a munaphiko nasamaja che
a loko kahe che ke jo ame pacha phari madina ja'isum to ijhajhatavala tyanthi apamanita lokone kadhi mukase, sambhalo ijhajhata to phakata allaha mate ja che, tena payagambara mate ane imanavala'o mate che, parantu a munaphiko janata nathi
He musalamano! Tamaru dhana ane tamari santana tamane allahana smaranathi vancita na kari de ane je avum karase te khuba ja nukasanamam hase
ane je kami pana ame tamane api rakhyum che temanthi (amara margamam) te pahela kharca karo ke tamara manthi ko'inum mrtyu tha'i jaya to te kaheva lage ke mara palanahara! Mane tum thodaka samayani chuta kema nathi apato? Ke hum sadako karum ane sadacari lokomam tha'i ja'u
ane jyare ko'ino nakki karela samaya avi pahonce che pachi tene allahata'ala kadapi chuta nathi apato ane je kami pana tame karo cho tene allaha ta'ala khuba ja sari rite jananara che
(dareka vastu'o) je akaso ane dharati para che allahani pavitratanum varnana kari rahi che, tenu ja samrajya che ane teni ja prasansa che ane te dareka vastu para saktimana che
tene ja tamaru sarjana karyu, ketalaka to tamara manthi inkari che ane ketalaka imanavala che ane je kami pana tame kari rahya cho allaha ta'ala khuba sari rite jovavalo che
tene ja akaso ane dharatine satyapurvaka peda kari, tene ja tamaro cahera banavya ane khuba ja sundara banavya ane teni ja tarapha pacha pharavanum che
te akasa ane dharati parani dareka vastune jane che ane je kami pana tame chupavo athava khullu karo te (darekane) jane che, allaha to hrdayoni vatone pana janavavalo che
sum tamari pase a pahelana inkari'oni vata nathi pahonci? Jemane potana karyoni saja cakhi lidhi ane jemana mate du:Khadayi yatana che
a etala mate ke temani pase temana payagambara khulla purava la'ine avya to te'o'e kahim didhu ke sum manavi amane margadarsana apase, basa! Inkara kari didho ane modhum pheravi lidhum ane allaha pana (temanathi) beparava tha'i gayo ane allaha to beniyajha, gunavana ja che
Te inkari'o'e vicari lidhu che ke biji vara jivita nahim karavamam ave, tame kahim do ke kema nahim? Allahana soganda! Tame cokkasa biji vara jivita karavamam avaso. Pachi je kami pana tame karyu che teni khabara (tamane) apavamam avase ane allaha mate a ghanum ja sarala che
to tame allaha para tena payagambara para ane te prakasa (kura'ana) para jene ame avatarita karyum che, imana lavo ane allaha ta'ala tamara dareka karyothi khabaradara che
je divase tamane saune te bhega thavana divase bhega karase, te ja a divasa che hara-jitano. Ane je vyakti allaha para imana lavi sadakaryo kare allaha tenathi teni bura'i'o dura kari dese. Ane tene jannatomam dakhala karase, jeni nice nahero vahi rahi che, jemam te'o hammesa hammesa rahese, a ja bhavya saphalata che
ane je loko'e inkara karyo ane amari ayatone juthalavi te ja (badha) jahannami che, (je'o) jahannamamam hammesa rahese. Te khuba ja kharaba thekanum che
ko'i paresani allaha ni raja vagara nathi avi sakati, je allaha para imana lave allaha tene satya margadarsana ape che ane allaha dareka vastune khuba ja janavavalo che
(loko) allahanum kahevum mano ane payagambaranum pana kahevum mano, basa! Jo tame modhum pheravo to amara payagambarana sire phakata spasta pahoncadi devanum che
allahana sivaya ko'i saco ma'abuda nathi ane imanavala'e phakata allaha para bharoso rakhavo jo'i'e
he imanavala'o! Tamari patni'o ane santano manthi ketalaka tamara satru che basa! Temanathi savadhana rahejo ane jo tame mapha kari do athava java do ane ksama kari do. To allaha ta'ala ksama karanara dayalu che
tamaru dhana ane santano kasoti che ane khuba ja motum valatara allaha pase che
Basa! Jyam sudhi tamarathi tha'i sake allahathi darata raho ane sambhalata ane ajnapalana karata raho ane allahana margamam kharca karata raho je tamara mate uttama che ane je vyakti potana manani lalacathi suraksita rakhavamam ave te ja saphala che
jo tame allahane uttama rna apaso (etale ke tena margamam kharca karaso) to te tene tamara mate vadharato rahese ane tamara gunaha pana mapha kari dese. Allaha khuba ja kadaradana ane sahanasila che
te chupi ane khulli (vatono) janavavalo che, prabhutvasali, hikamatavalo che
he payagambara! (Potani komane kaho) jyare tame potani patni'one talaka apava iccho to temani iddata (masikano samayagalo puro thaya pachi) mam temane talaka apo ane iddatana samayane yada rakho ane allaha ta'alathi darata raho je tamaro palanahara che, na tame temane potana gharo manthi kadho ane na to te (pote) nikale, ham te alaga vata che ke te spasta bura'i kari bese, a allahani nakki karela hada che, je vyakti allahani hadathi agala vadhi jaya tene kharekhara potana upara atyacara karyo, tame nathi janata, kadaca a pachi allaha ta'ala (mela-melapa) ni ko'i navi vata ubhi kari de
basa! Jyare a stri'o potani iddatani najika pahonci jaya to temane kayadapurvaka potana pase rakho, athava to kayadapurvaka temane alaga kari do ane eka-bija manthi ve vyakti'one saksi banavi lo ane allahane khusa karava mate sacci saksi apo. A ja che te jeni sikhamana temane apavamam ave che, je allaha ane kiyamatana divasa para imana rakhata hoya ane je vyakti allahathi dare che, allaha tena mate chutakarani sthiti ubhi kari de che
Ane tene evi jgya'ethi roji pahoncade che jeni tene kalpana pana na hoya ane ji vyakti allaha para bharoso karase, allaha tena mate purato che, allaha ta'ala potanum karya puru karene ja rahese, allaha ta'ala'e dareka vastuno eka andajo nakki kari rakhela che
tamari stri'o manthi je stri'o masikathi nirasa tha'i ga'i hoya, jo tamane sanka hoya to temano samayagalo trana mahina che ane temani pana jene masika avavanum saru pana na tha'i hoya, ane garbhavati stri'ono samayagalo temanum prasuti tha'i jaya tyam sudhi che. Ane je vyakti allaha ta'alathi darase allaha tena (dareka) karya sarala kari dese
a allahano adesa che, je tene tamari tarapha avatarita karyo che ane je vyakti allahathi darase allaha te'ona papa khatma kari dese ane tene khuba ja moto badalo apase
tame potani sakti pramane jyam raho cho tyam te (talakavali) stri'one rakho ane temane satavava mate takalipha na apo ane jo te garbhathi hoya to jyam sudhi balaka janme tyam sudhi temane kharca apata raho, phari jo tamara kahevathi te ja dudha pivadave to tame teni'one teno badalo api do ane eka-bijathi salahasucana kari lo ane jo tame andara andara jhaghado to tenina kahevathi ko'i biji (stri) dudha pivadavase
dhanavano'e potana dhana pramane kharca karavo jo'i'e ane jena para rojini tangi karavamam avi hoya tene jo'i'e ke je kami allaha ta'ala'e tene apyum che temanthi ja (potani sakti mujaba) ape, ko'ine pana allaha takalipha pahoncadato nathi parantu tetali ja jetali sahanasilata tene api che, allaha tangi pachi khusahali api dese
ane ketalika vasti'ovala'o'e potana palanaharana adeso ane tena payagambaroni avajna kari, to ame pana temano sakhata hisaba lidho ane te'one vana dekhi yatana api
Basa! Te'o'e potana karyoni maja cakhi lidhi ane chevate temanum nukasana ja thayum
te'o mate allaha ta'ala e sakhata yatana taiyara kari rakhi che. Basa! Allahathi daro he samajadara imanavala'o, ni:Sanka allaha e tamara tarapha sikhamana utari che
(etale ke) payagambara je tamane spasta allahana adeso padhi sambhalave che, jethi temane je'o imana lavya che ane sadakaryo kare che te'one andhakara manthi prakasa tarapha la'i ave. Ane je vyakti allaha para imana la'i ave ane sadakaryo kare, allaha te'one evi jannatomam dakhala karase jena nice nahero vahi rahi che, jemam te'o hammesa hammesa rahese, ni:Sanka allaha e tene uttama roji api che
allaha te che jene sata akaso banavya ane te ja pramane dharati pana. Teno adesa banneni vacce utare che, jethi tame jani lo ke allaha dareka vastu para saktimana che. Ane allaha ta'ala'e dareka vastune (potana) jnanamam gheri rakhi che
he payagambara! Je vastune allaha'e tamara mate halala kari didhi che, tene tame kema harama theravo cho? (Sum) tame potani patni'oni khusi prapta karava mango cho. Ane allaha ksama karavavalo,dayalu che
allaha'e tamara mate sogandone todavani (padhdhati) nakki karela che, ane allaha tamaro malika che ane te ja jananara, hikamatavalo che
ane yada karo jyare payagambare potani ketalika patni'one eka khanagi vata kahi, basa! Teni'e te vata kahim didhi ane allaha'e potana payagambarane teni jana kari, to payagambara'e thodika vatato kahi didhi ane thodika vatane tali didhi, pachi jyare payagambare potani te patnine a vata kahi to te kaheva lagi, ani khabara tamane kone api? Kahyum badhu ja jananara, dareka khabara rakhanara allaha'e mane jana kari
(He payagambarani banne patni'o) jo tame banne allaha same tauba kari lo (to ghanu ja saru che) ni:Sanka tamara dila jhuki padaya che ane jo tame payagambarana virodha ekabijani madada karaso (to jani lo) teno (payagambarano) madadagara allaha che ane jibra'ila che ane sadacari imanavala'o ane temana sivaya pharista'o pana madada karanara che
jo te (payagambara) tamane talaka api de to najikamam ja temane temano palanahara tamara badalamam tamarathi uttama patni'o melavase, je islamavali, imanavali, allaha ni same jhukavavali, tauba karavavali, bandagi karavavali, rojha rakhavavali hase, vidhava ane kumarika'o
he imanavala'o! Tame potane ane potana gharavala'one te agathi bacavo jenum indhana manavi'o ane pat'thara che, jena para sakhata dilavala, kdaka pharista'o nakki che, jemane je adesa allaha ape che teni avajna nathi karata, parantu je adesa apavamam ave che kari nakhe che
he inkari'o! Aje tame bahanum na karo, tamane phakata tamara karyono badalo apavamam ave che
he imanavala'o! Tame allahani samaksa sacci, nikhalasatathi tauba karo. Najika che ke tamaro palanahara tamara gunaha dura kari dem ane tamane evi jannatomam dakhala karase jeni nice nahero vahi rahi che, je divase allaha ta'ala payagambara ane imanavala'one je temani sathe che temane apamanita nahim kare. Temano prakasa temani same ane temani jamani baju'e pharase. Te'o du'a'o karata hase, he amara palanahara! Amane paripurna prakasa apa ane amane mapha kari dem. Kharekhara tum dareka vastu para saktimana che
he payagambara! Inkari'o ane munaphiko (dhongi'o) sathe jehada karo, ane te'o para sakhati karo, temanum thekanum jahannama che, ane te atyanta kharaba thekanum che
Allaha ta'ala'e inkari'o mate nuha ane luta a.Sa. Ni patni'onum udaharana bayana karyu, a banne amara banda'o manthi be sadacari banda'ona gharamam hati, pachi teni'o'e temani sathe visrvasaghata karyo, basa! Te banne (sadacari banda'o) temanathi allahani (ko'i yatana) na roki sakya ane adesa api devamam avyo (he stri'o) jahannama mam janara'o sathe tame banne pana jati raho
ane allaha ta'ala'e imanavala'o mate phira'auna ni patninum udaharana bayana karyu, jyare ke tene du'a kari ke he mara palanahara! Mara mate potani pase jannatamam ghara banavi de. Ane mane phira'auna ane tena (kharaba) karyothi bacavi le ane mane atyacari lokothi bacavi le
ane (udaharana apyum) imarana ni dikari marayamanum, jene potani pratisthani raksa kari, pachi ame amara taraphathi temam jiva phunki didho ane teni'e (marayama) potana palanaharani vato ane teni kitaboni pusti kari ane bandagi karanara'o manthi hati
khuba ja barakatavalo che te (allaha) jena hathamam saltanata che. Ane je dareka vastu'o para saktimana che
jene mrtyu ane jivanane te mate peda karyu ke tamari kasoti kare, ke tamara manthi kona sara karyo kare che. Ane te sarvopari (ane) ksama karanara che
jene sata akaso tala para tala banavya, (to e jovavala) allaha krpalu na sarjanamam ko'i avyavastha nahi ju'e, pharivara (najara thamavine) jo'i le sum ko'i tirada pana dekha'i che
pharivara be be vakhata jo'i le, tari najara tari tarapha apamanita (ane lacara) tha'ine thakine pachi pharase
ni:Sanka ame duniyana akasane diva'o (tara'o) vade sanagaryum ane temane saitanone maravanum madhyama banavi didhu ane saitano mate ame (jahannamani salagavi denari) yatana taiyara kari didhi
Ane potana palanaharano inkara karanara'o mate jahannamani yatana che ane te ketali kharaba jagya che
jyare temam te'o nakhavamam avase to teno khuba ja moto avaja sambhalase ane te josa mari rahi hase
najika che ke (hamana) krodhathi phati jase, jyare pana temam ko'i jutha nakhavamam avase tenathi jahannamana rakhevalo savala karase ke sum tamari pase khabaradara karanara ko'i nahato avyo
te javaba apase ke kema nahi, avyo hato, parantu ame temane juthalavya ane ame kahyum ke allaha ta'ala'e kasum pana utaryum nathi. Tame khuba ja mota geramarge cho
ane kahese ke agara ame sambhalata hota athava to samajya hota to jahannami'omam na hota
basa temane potanum papa svikari lidhum, have a jahannami'o dura tha'i java
ni:Sanka je loko potana palanaharathi vinadekhe darata rahe che temana mate ksama che ane bhavya savaba che
tame potani vatone chupavo athava to jahera karo, te to hrdayona bhedone pana khuba ja sari rite jane che
sum te ja na jane, jene sarjana karyu? Phari te khuba ja janakara che
te hasti jene tamara mate jaminane nimna ane ajnavarti banavi didhi, jethi tame tena rasta'o para harata pharata raho ane allahani rojimam thi kha'o (pi'o), teni ja tarapha (tamare) jivita tha'i ubhu thavanum che
sum tame e vatathi pana nirbhaya tha'i gaya cho ke akasovalo tamane jaminamam dhasavi de ane eka'eka jamina dagamagi jaya
athava sum tame a vatathi nirbhaya tha'i gaya cho ke akasovalo tamara para paththara varasavi de, pachi to tamane khabara padi ja jase ke mari cetavani kevi hati
ane temanathi pahelana loko'e pana juthalavyu, to temana para najara dodavo ke mari pakada kevi sakhata tha'i
Sum a loko potana upara phelayela ane (kayareka) sametayela (udata) pankhi'o ne nathi jota, temane (allaha) krpalu e ja (hava ane vatavaranamam) takavi rakhya che, ni:Sanka dareka vastu teni dekharekha hethala che
sivaya allahana tamaru te kevum laskara che, je tamari madada kari sake, inkari'o to kharekhara dhokamam ja che
agara allaha ta'ala tamari roji roki le to bata'o kona che je tamane phari roji apase? Parantu (inkari'o) to vidroha ane vimukhata para hathe cadhi gaya che
ham, te vyakti vadhu satyana marga upara che je undhum ghaline cali rahyo che, athava to te je satyana margane parakhine sidho calato hoya
kahi do! Ke te ja (allaha) che jene tamaru sarjana karyu ane tamara kana, ankho ane hrdaya banavya, tame khuba ja ocho abhara mano cho
kahi do! Ke te ja che jene tamane dharati para phelavi didha ane jeni tarapha tamane ekatha karavamam avase
(inkari'o) savala kare che ke te vacana kyare thase, agara tame saca hoya (to batavo)
tame kahi do! Ke tenum jnana to allahane ja che, hum to phakata spasta rite saceta karavavalo chum
jyare a loko te vacanane najika jo'i lese te vakhate te inkari'ona mukha bagadi jase ane kahi devamam avase ke a ja che jeni tame iccha karata hata
tame kahi do! Agara mane ane mara sathi'one allaha ta'ala nasta kari de, athava amara para daya kare, (banne paristhiti'omam evum to batavo) ke inkari'one du:Khadayi yatanathi kona bacavase
tame kahi do! Ke te ja krpalu che. Ame to tena para imana lavi cukaya ane tena para ja amaro visrvasa che. Tamane najikamam ja khabara padi jase ke nari pathabhrastatamam kona che
Tame kahi do! Ha e to batavo ke jo tamaru (pivanum) pani jaminamam jatum rahe to kona che je tamara mate vahetum pani lave
nuna, soganda che kalamana ane tena, je kami pana te (pharista'o) lakhe che
tame potana palanaharani krpathi pagala nathi
ane ni:Sanka tamara mate ananta badalo che
ane ni:Sanka tame khuba ja srestha (uttama) caritravala cho
basa! Have tame pana jo'i leso ane te'o pana jo'i lese
ke tamaramam thi kona pralobhanamam sapadayelu che
ni:Sanka tamaro palanahara potana margathi bhatakelane khuba ja sari rite jane che, ane te sanmargi'o ne pana khuba ja sari rite jane che
basa! Tame juthalavanara'oni (vata) na mano
te'o to icche che ke tame thodaka narama pado to te'o pana narama padi jaya
ane tame ko'i eva vyaktinum pana kahevum na manaso je vadhare soganda khavavalo
be'abaru, nica, mahenantona maranara, cadi khanara
bhala'ithi rokavavalo, atireka karanara, papi
atada svabhavano, sathe sathe badanama pana che
teno vidroha phakata etala mate che ke te dhana-sampatti valo ane santanovalo che
jyare teni same amari ayato padhavamam ave che to kahi de che ke a to aga'una lokoni varta'o che
ame pana teni sundha (naka) para dama apisum
ni:Sanka ame temani tevi ja rite kasoti kari jevi rite ke ame bagicavala'o ni kasoti kari hati. Jyare ke temane soganda khadhi ke vaheli parodha thata ja a bagicana phala todi la'isum
ane in sa'a allaha na bolya
basa! Temana para tara palanahara taraphathi eka aphata careya bajuthi phari vali ane te su'i ja rahya hata
basa! Te bagico evo tha'i gayo jevi ke vadheli paka
have savara thata ja temane ekabijane pokarya
Ke agara tamare phala todava hoya to potani kheti para vaheli parodhamam cali nikalo
phari te loko dhire-dhire vato karata nikalya
ke ajana divase ko'i lacara tamari pase na avi sake
ane lapakata savara savaramam nikalya (samaji rahya hata) ke ame samartha chi'e (phala todava mate)
jyare temane bagico joyo to kaheva lagya, ni:Sanka ame rasto bhuli gaya
na na, parantu apanum bhagya phuti gayu
te lokomam je srestha hato tene kahyu ke hum tamane nahato kaheto ke tame allaha ni pavitratanum varnana kema nathi karata
to badha ja kaheva lagya, apano palanahara pavitra che, ni:Sanka ame ja atyacari hata
phari te'o eka-bija tarapha pharine eka-bijane thapako apava lagya
kaheva lagya khuba aphasosa! Kharekhara ame vidrohi hata
um'mida che ke amaro palanahara amane anathi saro badalo apase, ame to have potana palanaharathi ja apeksa kari'e chi'e
avi ja rite musibata ave che. Ane akhirata (paraloka) ni musibata ghani ja moti che. Kadaca te'o janata hota
daranara'o mate temana palanahara pase ne'amatovali jannato che
sum ame musalmanone papi'o jeva kari da'isum
tamane sum tha'i gayu, keva nirnayo karo cho
sum tamari pase ko'i kitaba che je tame padhata hoya
ke temam tamari manacahi vato hoya
athava to tame amarathi ketalika sogando lidhi che? Je kayamata (pralaya) sudhi rahe, ke tamara mate te badhu ja che je tame potani taraphathi nakki kari lo
temane pucho ke temana manthi kona a vatano javabadara (davedara) che
sum temana ko'i bhagidara che? To pota potana bhagidaro la'i ave, agara te'o saca che
Je divase pindali (dhicana no nicalo bhaga) kholi nakhavamam avase ane sijado karava mate bolavavamam avase. To (sijado) nahi kari sake
najaro nici hase ane temana para kalanka chava'i rahyu hase. Tema chanta a sijada mate (te vakhate pana) bolavavamam avata hata jyare ke tandurasta hata
basa! Mane ane a kalamane juthalavanara'one chodi do, ame temane ama dhire dhire khencisum ke temane khabara pana nahim pade
ane hum temane dhila apisa, ni:Sanka mari yojana sakhata sacota che
sum tame temanathi ko'i valatara iccho cho jena dandana boja hethala daba'i rahya hoya

basa! Tame potana palanaharana adesani dhiraja thi (raha ju'o), ane machalivala (arthat murada eka payagambara che jemanum nama yunusa a.Sa. Che, te'o potana loko pasethi allahano adesa avya pahela ja samudra tarapha calya gaya. Tyam te'one temani bhulano pasatavo thayo. Pasatavo thanta ja temane pote samudramam chalanga lagavi ane tyam te'one eka machali'e lagabhaga divasa sudhi potana petamam rakhela) jeva na tha'i java, jyare ke tene sokatura tha'i du'a kari
agara tene tena palanaharani madada na avi hota to ni:Sanka te kharaba paristhitimam sapata medana para nakhi devamam avata
tene tena palanahare phari pasanda kari lidho ane tene sadacari lokomansamela kari didho

sabita thavavali
sabita thavavali sum che
ane tane sum khabara ke te sabita thanara sum che
Te khakhadavi denarane samuda ane ada (pracina samayani takatavara kaumo'e) juthalavi didhi
(jena parinama rupe) samudane trasajanaka (ane unca) avaja vade nasta karavamam avya
ane ada ne tivra tophani andhithi nasta kari devamam avya
jene temana para nirantara sata ratri'o ane atha divasa sudhi (allaha'e) chavayeli rakhi. Basa! Tame jota ke a loko jamina para evi rite patakayela padaya che jevi rite ke khajurana khokhala thada hoya
sum temana manthi ko'i pana tamane baki dekha'i che
phira'auna ane tenathi pahelana loko ane jemani vasti'o palatavi nakhi temane pana aparadha acaryo
ane potana palanaharana payagambarani avaganana kari. (Chevate) allaha e te'one (pana) sakhata pakadamam la'i lidha
jyare panimam tophana avi gayum to te samaye ame tamane naukamam savara kari didha
jethi te tamara mate sikhamana ane yadagara bani jaya ane (jethi) yada rakhavavala kana tene yada rakhe
basa! Jyare suramam eka phunka maravamam avase
ane jamina tatha parvato uthavi levamam avase. Ane eka ja praharamam curecura kari devamam avase
te divase tha'i janari (kayamata) tha'i jase
ane akasa phati jase, ane te divase ghanum ja nabalu padi jase
tena kinara'o para pharista'o hase, ane tara palanaharano arsa te divase atha (pharista'o) potana upara uthavela hase
te divase tame sau raju karavamam avaso, tamaru ko'i rahasya chupayelum nahi rahe
to, jene tenum karmapatra jamana hathamam apavamam avase, to te kaheva lagase ke lo maru karmapatra vanci lo
mane to sampurna visrvasa hato ke mane maro hisaba malase ja
basa! Te eka managamata jivanamam hase
ucca darajjavali jannatamam
jena guccha nami padela hase
(Temane kahevamam avase) ke anandathi kha'o pi'o, potana te karmona badalamam je tame vitela divasomam karya
parantu jenum karmapatra tena daba hathamam apavamam avase to te kahase ke kadaca mane maru karmapatra apavamam ja na avyu hota
ane hum janato ja na hota ke hisaba sum che
kadaca! Ke mrtyu (maru) kama puru kari deta
maru dhana pana mane kami phayado na pahoncadi sakyu

adesa apavamam avase, tene pakadi lo pachi tene galiyum paheravi do
pachi tene dojhakhamam nakhi do
pachi tene evi sankalamam bandhi do jeni mapani sittera hatha lambi che

ane lacarane khavadavava mate protsahana nahato apato

(a to) jagatana palanahare avatarita karela che

basa! Tu potana mahana palanaharani pavitrata bayana kara
eka savala karanara'e te yatana vise savala karyo, je spasta thanari che

basa! Tu sari rite dhiraja rakha

(parantu) ekabijane dekhadi devamam avase, gunegara te divasani yatanana badalamam muktidanda rupe potana dikara'one

ane potana kutumbi'one, je tene asaro apata hata
ane dharati paranam saune apava icchase jethi te'o tene chutakaro apavi de
(parantu) kadapi avum nahim thaya, ni:Sanka te bhadakati (aga) che

ane bhegu karine sambhali rakhe che

ha! Temani patni'o ane bandi'o vise jemana te'o malika che, temana para ko'i dosa nathi

te vata para ke te'ona badale temanathi sara lokone la'i avi'e ane ame aksama nathi
basa! Tu emane ladata-jhaghadata ane khelakuda karata chodi de ahim sudhi ke potana te divasathi mulakata kari le jenum temane vacana apavamam avyu che
je divase a loko kabaromanthi dodata nikalase, jevi rite ke te'o ko'i jgya tarapha jhadapathi ja'i rahya hoya
temani ankho nameli hase, temana para badanami chavayeli hase. A che te divasa jenum temane vacana apavamam avyu hatum
ni:Sanka ame nuha (a.Sa.) Ne temani koma tarapha moklya ke potani komane daravi do (ane saceta kari do) te pahela ke temani pase du:Khadayi yatana avi jaya
(nuha a.Sa.E) kahyu, ke aya mari koma! Hum tamane spasta rite cetavani apanara chum
Ke tame allahani bandagi karo ane tenathi ja daro. Ane maru kahyu mano
to te tamara gunaha mapha kari dese ane tamane eka nisrcita samaya sudhi chuta apase. Ni:Sanka jyare allaha ta'alanum vacana avi jaya che, to dhila nathi apato. Kadaca ke tamane budhdhi hota
(nuha a.Sa.E) kahyu, aya mara palanahara! Mem potani komane rata divasa tari (bandagi) tarapha bolavya
parantu mara bolavava para a loko vadhu dura java lagya
mem jyare pana temane tari ksama tarapha bolavya, temane potani angali'o potana kanomam nakhi didhi ane potana kapadathi (modhum) dhanki didhu. Ane jida kari ane khuba ja ghamanda karyu
pachi mem temane unca avaje bolavya
ane ni:Sanka mem temane jaheramam pana kahyu ane gupta rite pana
ane mem kahyu, ke potana palanaharathi potana gunahani maphi mango, te kharekhara khuba ja ksama karavavalo che
te tamara para akasamanthi khuba ja (varasada) varasavase
ane tamane khuba ja dhana ane santano apase. Ane tamane bagica'o apase ane tamara mate nahera vahavi dese
tamane sum tha'i gayu che ke tame allaha ni mahanata nathi manata
jo ke tene tamane vibhinna rite banavya che
sum tame nathi jota ke allaha ta'ala'e tala para tala kevi rite sata akaso banavya
ane temam candrane khuba ja prakasita banavyo, ane surajane prakasita dipaka
ane tamane jaminathi eka (visesa dekharekha hethala) ugadaya. (Etale ke sarjana karyu)
phari tamane temam ja parata karase ane (eka khasa rite) phari kadhase
ane kharekhara tamara mate dharatine allaha ta'ala'e patharanum banavi didhu che
jethi tame tena khulla rasta'o para haro-pharo
Nuha (a.Sa.) E kahyu ke aya mara palanahara! Te loko'e mari vatane rada kari, ane teva lokoni vata mani jemanum dhana ane santano'e temani khotamam (kharekhara) vadharo karyo
ane te loko'e bhare dhoko karyo
ane temane kahyu ke tame kadapi potana pujyone na chodaso, ane na vadda, suva'a, ane yagusa ane ya'uka ane nasra ne (chodaso)
ane temane ghana lokone pathabhrasta karya, (aya allaha) tu te atyacari'oni pathabhrastatane vadhu kara
a loko potana papona lidhe dubadi devamam avya ane jahannamamam pahoncadi devamam avya. Ane allaha sivaya temane ko'i madada karanara na joyo
ane nuha (a.Sa.) E kahyu, ke aya mara palanahara! Tum jamina para ko'i inkarine vasavavalo na chodisa
jo tu temane chodi da'isa to (ni:Sanka) a loko tara banda'one (pana) bhatakavi dese. Ane duracari ane inkari'one ja janma apase
aya mara palanahara! Tu mane ane mara mata-pita ane je imanani sthitimam mara gharamam avya ane dareka momina puruso ane stri'one mapha kari de ane inkari'one barabadi sivaya biji ko'i vatamam agala na vadharisa
(muham'mada sa.A.Va.) Tame kahi do ke mane vahi karavamam avi che ke jinnatona eka juthe (kura'ana) sambhalyu ane kahyu ke ame ad- bhuta kura'ana sambhalyu che
je sidha marga tarapha margadarsana kare che. Ame tena para imana la'i avya. (Have) ame kadapi ko'ine pana potana palanaharano bhagidara nahi theravi'e
ane ni:Sanka amara palanaharanum gaurava khuba ja ucca che. Na tene ko'ine (potani) patni banavi ane na to dikaro
ane e ke apanamam no murkha allaha vise satya virudhdha vata
ane ame to evum ja samajata rahya ke sakya nathi ke manavi ane jinnata allaha para jutha race
Vata evi che ke ketalaka manavi'o ketalaka jinnatothi sarana mangata hata. Jenathi jinnato potani pathabhrastatamam vadhi gaya
ane (manavi'o) e pana jinnato jevum anumana karyu hatu ke allaha ko'ine pana nahim mokale. (Athava to ko'ine bijivara jivita nahim kare)
ane ame akasane cakasyum to tene sakhata cokidaro ane sakhata angara'o thi chavayelu joyu
te pahela ame vato sambhalava mate akasamam jgya'e jgya'e besi jata hata, have je pana kana lagave che te eka angarane potani lagamam ju'e che
ame nathi janata ke dharativala'o sathe ko'i kharaba vartanano irado che athava temana palanaharano irado temani sathe bhala'ino che
ane e ke (ni:Sanka) ketalaka to amaramam sadacari'o che. Ane ketalaka tena virudhdha pana che, ame vividha rite vahencayela chi'e
ane ame samaji lidhu ke ame allaha ta'alane dharati para kadapi aksama nahi kari saki'e ane na ame dodine tene haravi saki'e chi'e
ame to satya margani vata sambhalata ja tena para imana lavya ane je pana potana palanahara para imana lavase, tene na ko'i nukasana no bhaya hase ane na to atyacarano
ha! Amaramanthi ketalaka to musalamana che ane ketalaka an'yayi che. Basa! Je ajnakari tha'i gaya temane satya marga sodhi lidho
ane je atyacari'o che te jahannamanum indhana banase
ane (he nabi evum pana kahi do) ke jo loko satya marga para sidha calata to kharekhara ame temane puskala matramam pani pivadavata
jethi ame temani kasoti kari'e ane je vyakti potana palanaharana smaranathi modhum pheravi lese to allaha ta'ala tene sakhata yatanamam nakhi dese
ane masjido phakata allaha mate ja che. Basa! Allaha ta'ala sathe ko'i an'ya ne na pokaro
Ane jyare allahano bando teni bandagi mate ubho thayo to najikamam ja juthana jutha teni upara tuti padaya
tame kahi do ke hum to phakata mara palanaharane ja pokaru chum ane teni sathe ko'ine pana bhagidara nathi theravato
kahi do ke hum tamara ko'i nukasana ane phayadano adhikara dharavato nathi
kahi do ke mane kadapi ko'i allahathi nahi bacavi sake ane mane kadapi
parantu (marum kama) allahani vata ane tena adeso (loko sudhi) pahoncadi devanu che, (have) je pana allaha ane tena payagambaranum kahyum nahim mane, tena mate jahannama ni aga che. Jemam ava loko hammesa rahese
(temani ankha nahim khule) ahim sudhi ke tene jo'i le, jenum vacana temane apavamam ave che, basa! Najikamam ja jani lese ke kona madadagara nirbala ane konum jutha ochum che
kahi do ke mane khabara nathi ke jenum vacana tamane apavamam ave che, te najika che athava maro palanahara tena mate durano samaya nakki karase
te adrsyane janavavalo che ane te potana adrsyani jana ko'ine karato nathi
sivaya te payagambarana, jene te pasanda kari le, parantu teni agala-pachala pana cokidara nakki kari de che
jethi temana palanaharana adesone pahoncadavani jana tha'i jaya, allaha ta'ala'e temani ajubaju (ni dareka vastu'o) ne gheramam la'i rakhi che ane dareka vastune gani rakhela che

ratri (na samaye namajha) mam ubha tha'i java parantu ochum
adadhi rata athava to tenathi pana thodum ochum kari do
athava to tenathi thodu vadhari do ane kura'ana ruki rukine (spasta) padhaya kara
ni:Sanka ame tamara para khuba ja bhare vata najikamam ja utarisum
ni:Sanka ratamam uthavum mana upara kabu melavava mate khuba ja asarakaraka che ane vatane yogya kari devanum karana che
Hakikatamam tamane divasabhara ghani ja vyastata hoya che
tame potana palanaharana namanum smarana karata raho ane dareka sarjani'othi kapa'ine teni ja tarapha dhyana dhari do
purva ane pasrcimano palanahara jena sivaya ko'i ma'abuda (bandagine layaka) nathi, tame tene ja potano karyasadhaka banavi lo
ane je ka'im te kahe tena para dhairya rakho ane sajjanatapurvaka temanathi juda tha'i java
mane ane te juthalavanara khusahala lokone chodi do ane temane thodika mahetala api do
ni:Sanka amari pase sakhata sankalo che ane bhalake balati jahannama che
ane galamam phasa'i janara khoraka che ane du:Khadayi yatana che
je divase dharati ane parvato dhruji uthase ane parvato vikherayeli reti jeva bani jase
ni:Sanka ame tamari tarapha pana tamara para saksi apanara payagambara mokali didha che. Jevum ke ame phira'auna tarapha payagambara mokalya hata
to phira'aunane te payagambarani vata na mani to ame tene sakhata (sajamam) pakadi lidha
jo tame inkari rahya, to te divase kevi rite sarana pamaso je divasa balakone vrdhdha kari devamam avase
je divase akasa phati padase, allaha ta'alanum a vacana tha'ine ja rahase
ni:Sanka a sikhamana che, basa! Je icche te potana palanahara tarapha jato marga apanavi lem
Tamaro palanahara sari rite jane che ke tame ane tamara sathenum eka jutha lagabhaga be-trtiyansa rata ane adadhi rata athava eka- trtiyansa ratamam tahajjuda (modi ratre padhavamam avati namajha) padhe che. Ane rata divasano hisaba allaha ta'ala pase ja che, te (khuba) ja jane che ke tame tene kadapi pali nahi sako basa! Tene tamara para krpa kari, jethi jetalum kura'ana padhavum tamara mate sarala hoya tetalum ja padho. Te jane che ke tamaramanthi ketalaka bimara pana hase, ketalaka bija dharati para hari-pharine allaha ta'alani krpa (etale ke roji) pana sodhase ane ketalaka loko allaha ta'alana rastamam jihada (dharmika yudhdha) pana karase, to tame jetalum kura'ana saralatathi padhi sako padho ane namajha pabandithi padhata raho ane jhakata (dharmadana) apata raho ane allaha ta'alane saru rna apo ane je sadakarya tame tamara mate agala mokalaso tene allaha ta'alane tyam ati'uttama ane badalamam khubaja vadhare pamaso, allaha ta'ala pase ksama mangata raho, ni:Sanka allaha ta'ala ksama karanara krpavalo che

chevate tara palanahare temana para yatanano korado varasavi didho
hakikatamam taro palanahara takamam che
manusya (a sthiti che ke) teno palanahara jyare teni pariksa le che ane ijhajhata ape che, ane tene khusahali ape che, to te kaheva lage che, mara palanahare maru sanmana karyum
ane jyare te teni pariksa le che ane teni roji tanga kari de che, to te kaheva lage che ke mara palanahare marum apamana karyum
avum kadapi nahim! Parantu (vata evi che) ke tame (ja) loko anathano adara nathi karata
ane garibone khavadavava mate eka-bijane ubharata nathi
ane varasani sampatti sametine hadapa kari ja'o cho
ane dhanathi khuba prema karo cho
kadapi nahim, jyare dharati kuti-kutine barabara kari devamam avase
Ane tamaro palanahara (pote) avi jase ane pharista'o katarabandha avase
ane je divase jahannama pana lavavamam avase
e kahese ke kadaca! Mem potana a jivana mate pahela kami mokalyum hota
basa aje allahana ajhaba jevo ajhaba ko'ino nahim hoya
na tena jevi jakada ko'ini jakada hase
o santosi jiva
tum potana palanahara tarapha cala, evi rite ke tum tenathi prasanna, te tara thi prasanna
basa mara srestha banda'o mam dakhala tha'i ja
ane pravesi ja mari jannatamam
hum a saherana soganda kha'um chum
ane tame a saheramam raho cho
ane (soganda che) manavi'o na pita ane santanana
ni:Sanka ame manavinum (khuba ja) kastamam sarjana karyu che
sum te ema dhare che ke tena para ko'i kabu nahim pame
kaheto (phare) che ke mem to puskala dhana vedaphi nakhyum
sum (ema) samaje che ke ko'i'e tene joyo (pana) nathi
sum ame teni banne ankho nathi banavi
ane jibha ane hotha (nathi banavya)
ame dekhadi didha tene banne marga
parantu tenathi ghatimam pasara thavanum na tha'i sakayum
ane sum khabara padi ke ghati sum che
ko'i gala (bandi- bandi'o) ne mukta karavavum
athava to bhukhamara na divase bhojana karavavum
ko'i sambadhi'o mam na anatha ne
athava to rajhalata gariba ne
phari te loko manthi tha'i jato je'o imana lavya ane eka-bija ne dhiraja ane daya dakhavavani bhalamana kare che
a ja loko che jamani baju vala (khusahala loko)
ane je loko'e amari ayatono inkara karyo te du:Khi loko che
te ja loko para aga hase. Careva bajuthi ghereli hase
soganda che suryana tatha tena tadakana
soganda che cadrana jyare teni pachala ave
Soganda che divasana jyare suryane pragata kare
soganda che ratrina jyare tene dhaki dem
soganda che akasana ane tena sarjanana
soganda che dharatina ane tene barabara karavana
soganda che atmana ane tene thika-thaka karavana
phari samaja api tene bura'ini ane bhala'ini
jene tene pavitra kari te saphala thayo
ane jene tene melu karyu te nisphala thayo
(koma) samude potana vidrohana karane juthalavyum
jyare temana mam no moto durbhagi ubho thayo
temane allaha na payagambare kahi didhu hatum ke allaha ta'alani untani'ane teni pivanivari ni (suraksa karo)
te loko'e potana payagambara ne jutho samaji te untani na hatha-paga kapi nakhya. Basa! Temana palanahare temana gunahona karane temana upara prakopa utaryo. Ane pachi prakopane samana kari didho. Ane te abadine sapata kari didhi
te nathi darato tena vinasi parinamathi
soganda che ratrina jyare chava'i jaya
soganda che divasa na jyare prakasita thaya
soganda che te hastina jene nara ane madanum sarjana karyu
ni:Sanka tamaro prayasa vividha prakarano che
jene apyum (allahana rastamam) ane daryo (potana palanahara thi)
ane sadavatoni prsthi karato rahase
to ame pana tene sarala rastani sahulata kari da'isum
parantu jene kanjusi kari ane beparavahi dakhavi
ane sadavatone juthalavi
to ame pana teni tangi ane muskelino samana sarala kari da'isum
tenum dhana tene (undha) padati vakhate kasum kama nahim lage
ni:Sanka rasto batavavo amara sire che
ane amara ja hathamam che akhirata ane duniya
mem to tamane bhadake balati agathi saceta kari didha che
Jemam phakata te ja vidrohi dakhala thase
jene juthalavyum ane (tena anusaranathi) modhum pheravi lidhum
ane tenathi evo vyakti dura rakhavamam avase je khuba ja sanyami hase
je pavitra thava mate potanum dhana ape che
ko'ino tena para ko'i upakara nathi ke jeno badalo apavamam avato hoya
parantu phakata potana palanahara ijhajhatavala tatha sarvocca ni prasannata prapta karava mate
ni:Sanka te (allaha pana) najikamam raji tha'i jase
soganda che prakasita samayanam
ane soganda che ratrina jyare chava'i jaya
na to tara palanahare tane chodayo che, ane na to te kantalyo che
nisrcitapane tamara mate parinama saru'ata karata uttama hase
tamane tamaro palanahara khuba najikamam (phala) apase ane tame khusa tha'i jaso
sum tene tamane anatha jo'i sarana na apyum
ane tamane margathi ajana jo'i margadarsana na apyum
ane tamane nirdhana jo'i dhanavana na banavi didha
basa! Tame anatha sathe kathora vyavahara na karo
ane na mangavavala ne dhutkaro
ane potana palanaharani krpanum varnana karata raho
sum ame tamari chati nathi kholi nakhi
ane tamara para thi tamaro bhara ame utari didho
jene tamari pitha todi didhi hati
ane ame tamara smaranane unnati api
basa! Ni:Sanka tangini sathe saralata che
cokkasapane tangini sathe saralata che
basa jyare tame paravari java to bandagi mam mahenata karo
ane potana palanahara tarapha ja magna tha'i java
soganda che anjira ane jetunana
ane ture sinin na (eka parvata num nama)
ane te santivala saherana
ni:Sanka ame manavinum sarvottama svarupamam sarjana karyu
pachi tene nica mam nico kari didho
Parantu je loko imana lavya ane (pachi) sadakaryo karya to temana mate evo badalo che je kadi khatma nahim thaya
basa! Tane badalana divasane juthalavava para ka'i vastu ubhare che
sum allaha ta'ala (badha) nirnayakarta'o no nirnayakarta nathi
padho potana palanaharana namathi jene sarjana karyu
jene manavinum jami gayela lohithi sarjana karyu
tame padhata raho taro palanahara atyanta udara che
jene pena maraphate (jnana) sikhavadayum
jene manavine te sikhavadayum jene te na janato hato
kharekhara manavi to vidrohi bani rahyo che
etala mate ke te potane bedarakara (khusahala) samaje che
kharekhara pacha pharavum tara palanahara tarapha che
tene pana te joyo je bandane atakave che
jyare ke te bando namajha padhe che
sum bata'o to, te satya marga tarapha hoya
athava to sanyamatano adesa apato hoya
tamaro sum khyala che, agara a juthalavato hoya ane modhum pheravato hoya to
sum tene nathi janyum ke allaha ta'ala tene jo'i rahyo che
kadapi nahim, agara a bacato na rahyo to ame tena kapalana vala pakadine khencisum
evu kapala je juththu papi che
te potana tekedarone bolavi le
ame pana (jahannamana) rakhevalane bolavi la'isum
savadhana! Teni vata kadapi na manaso. Ane sajado karo,ane nikata tha'i ja'o
ni:Sanka ame a (kura'ana) ne kadrani ratamam utaryu
tane sum khabara ke kadrani rata sum che
kadrani rata eka hajara mahina'o thi uttama che
te (ratamam dareka karya) karava mate potana palanaharana adesathi pharista'o ane ruha (jibra'ila) utare che
a ratri sampurna salamati vali hoya che ane parodhana udaya sudhi (rahe che)
Granthavala'o mam na inkari'o ane musarika loko jyam sudhi temani pase spasta dalila na avi jaya atakanara na hata (te dalila a hati ke)
allaha ta'alano eka payagambara je pavitra grantha padhe
jemam saca ane thosa adeso hoya
granthavala'o potani pase khulli dalila avi gaya pachi pana (matabheda karine) alaga-alaga tha'i gaya
temane ana sivaya bijo ko'i adesa apavamam na avyo ke phakata allahani upasana kare. Tena mate ja dina ne visudhdha rakhe. Ibrahima hanipha na dina upara ane namajhane kayama kare. Ane jhakata apata rahe. A ja che dina saca panthano
ni:Sanka je loko granthavala'o manthi inkari thaya ane musarika, sau jahannamani agamam (jase) jyam te'o hammesa rahese. A loko dustatama sarjana che
ni:Sanka je loko imana lavya ane sadakarmo karya a loko sresthatama sarjana che
temanum phala temana palanahara pase hammesa rahenari jannato che, jemani nice nahero vahi rahi che. Jemam te'o hammesahammesa rahese. Allaha ta'ala temana thi khusa thayo ane te tenathi khusa thaya. A che tena mate je potana palanahara thi dare
jyare jamina purepuri halavi nakhavamam avase
ane jamina potano boja bahara kadhi phenki dese
manavi kaheva lagase ke ane sum tha'i gayu
te divase jamina potani dareka vatonum varnana kari dese
etala mate ke tara palanahare tene adesa apyo hase
te divase loko alaga-alaga samuha banine (pacha) pharase. Jethi temane temana karma batavavamam ave
basa! Jene rajabhara bhala'i kari hase, te tene jo'i lese
ane jene rajabhara bura'i kari hase, te tene jo'i lese
hamphata dodanara ghoda'ona soganda
pachi tapa marine angara kheranara'ona soganda
pachi vaheli savare chapa maranarana soganda
Basa! Te vakhate dhulani damari'o udave che
pachi teni sathe lasakarana tolamam ghusi jaya che
kharekhara manavi potana palanahara no khuba ja apakari che
ane ni:Sandeha te svayam tena para saksi che
te malana monha mam pana sakhata che
sum tene te samaya ni khabara nathi jyare kabaro mam je (kami) che, kadhi levamam avase
ane hrdayo ni chupi vato kadhi nakhavamam avase
cokkasapane temano palanahara te divase temani avasthathi vakepha hase
khatakhatavi nakhanara
sum che te khatakhatavi nakhanara
tane sum khabara te khatakhatavi nakhanara sum che
je divase manavi vikharayela patangiyani maphaka tha'i jase
ane parvato pinjayela rangina una jeva tha'i jase
pachi jena palla bhare hase
to te'o manapasanda esa'arama mam hase
ane jena palla'o halka hase
temanum thekanum haviyaha che
tane sum khabara ke te sum che
bhadake balati aga (che)
vadhu praptini ghelacha'e tamane bedhyana kari didha
etale sudhi ke tame kabara sudhi pahonci gaya
kadapi nahim, tame najikamam jani leso
kadapi nahim, phari tame tunka samayamam jani leso
kadapi nahim, agara tame kharekhara jani lo
to ni:Sanka tame jahannama jo'i leso
ane tame tene visrvasaniya ankhathi jo'i leso
phari te divase tamarathi cokkasapane krpa vise puchatacha thase
jamanana soganda
ni:Sanka (cokkasapane) manavi kharekhara nukasanamam che
sivaya te lokona je'o imana lavya, ane sara karyo karya ane (jemane) ekabijane satyanum sucana karyu, ane ekabija ne dhairyani sikhamana kari
moto vinasa che te dareka vyakti mate je mena-tona maranara, ninda karava valo hoya
je dhana ekathum karato jaya ane ganato jaya
Te samaje che ke tenum dhana teni pase hammesa rahese
kadapi nahim, a to jarura todi phodi nakhanara agamam nakhi devamam avase
ane tane sum khabara ke a aga kevi hase
te allaha ta'ala'e bhadakaveli aga hase
je hrdayo para cadhati jase
te temana upara badhi bajuthi bandha kareli hase
mota mota stambhomam
sum tame na joyum, ke tamara palanahare hathivala'o sathe sum karyu
sum temani yuktine nisphala na kari didhi
ane temana upara paksi'ona tole-tola mokali didha
je temane mati ane pat'tharani kankari'o mari rahya hata
basa! Temane khadhela bhusa jeva kari nakhya
kuraisi'o mam sokha utpanna thavane karane
(etale ke) temane siyala ane unalana sapharathi teva'i java mate, (tena upakara mam)
basa! Temane jo'i'e ke te ja ghara na palanaharani bandagi karata rahe
jene temane bhukhamara mam khavadavyum, ane dara (bhaya) mam santi (ane nisrcintata) api
sum tame (tene pana) joyo je badalana divasane juthalave che
a ja te che je anathane dhakka mare che
ane garibane khavadavavanum protsahana nathi apato
te namajhi'o mate kheda che (ane vaila namani jahannamani jagya) che
je potani namajhathi beparavaha che
je dekhado kare che
ane saman'ya jaruriyatathi roke che
ni:Sanka ame tamane (haujha) kausara (ane ghanum badhu) apyum che
basa! Tu potana palanahara mate namajha padha ane kurabani kara
kharekhara tamaro satru ja varasadara vagarano che, ane badanama che
tame kahi do ke aya inkari'o
na hum bandagi karu chum teni, jeni tame bandagi karo cho
na tame bandagi karavana cho teni, jeni hum bandagi karu chum
ane na hum bandagi karisa, jeni tame bandagi karo cho
Ane na tame teni bandagi karavana cho, jeni hum bandagi kari rahyo chum
tamara mate tamaro dina che ane mara mate maro dina che
jyare allahani madada ane vijaya avi jaya
ane tame lokone allahana dinamam tole-tola avata jo'i lo
tame potana palanaharani tasbiha (gunagana) mam lagi java, prasansa sathe ane tenathi ksamani du'a manga, ni:Sanka te khuba ja ksama kabula karavavalo che
abu lahaba na banne hatha tuti gaya ane te (pote) barabada tha'i gayo
na to tenum dhana tena mate kama avyum ane na to teni kamani
te najikamam bhadakaveli agamam jase
ane teni patni pana (jase) je lakadi'o uthavanari che
tena galamam kathinum doradum hase
tame kahi do ke te allaha ta'ala eka ja che
allaha ta'ala beniyajha che. (Evi hasti ke dareka sarjanane teni jarura che, tene ko'ini jarura nathi)
na tenathi ko'i peda thayu ane na te ko'ina thi peda thayo
ane na ko'i teni sarakhamaninum che
tame kahi do! Ke hum savarana palanaharani saranamam avum chum
dareka te vastuni bura'ithi je tene peda kari
ane andhari ratrini bura'ithi jyare tenum andharu phelaya jaya
ane gantha (lagavine te) mam phunkanarani bura'ithi (pana)
ane irsa karanara'o ni bura'ithi jyare te irsa kare
tame kahi do! Ke hum lokona palanaharani saranamam avum chum
lokona malikana (ane)
lokona ma'abudana (saranamam)
sanka'o nakhanara, pacha hati janarani bura'ithi
je lokona hrdayomam sanka'o nakhe che
(pachi) te jinnatomam thi hoya athava to manusyomam thi
